< review>
Doctor Scott is the best. I was in so much pain due to my wisdom teeth coming out. I normally go to western dental for checkup, but the waits are ridiculous, long, and very low quality, not to mention how they refused to take my wisdom teeth out because apparently my lower left was sitting on my main nerve. So for the next 2 years I kept ignoring, terrified that if I did take them out I would loose sensation in my mouth.

Just a few days ago I was having terrible pain and wouldn‚Äôt go away. I knew I could not ignore it anymore and had to get them remove ASAP! So I started looking into other local dentist offices and the also said they could not remove them because with the nerve things would be too risky.

So almost in tears from the pain, my boyfriend recommended me doctor Scott‚Äôs Fross and I was like sure why not give it a try. During that appointment I got an X-ray and spoke to Dr. Scott about where I stood. He was very knowledgeable and made me feel completely comfortable and safe. Our discussion was literally about 15 minutes, he went over the process and assure me that he would be able to remove them with no problem... plus gave me a prescription for pain, infection, and inflammation.

< review>
We were looking for a dog-friendly winery with great wine and a great vibe - and we couldn't have picked a better place to visit than Cosentino!  Their tasting room is awesome - lots of seating and a very cool rustic chic - lots of wood and concrete floors.  The wine is SO good... across the board we were very impressed (and it is VERY affordable!).  My fav was the Sangiovese!  But the very best thing about Cosentino is the people - so friendly and incredibly knowledgeable about the wine.  My dog just loved that she was immediately showered with treats and her own water bowl!    We can't wait to come back again!</review>

<Time>1509035490950< /Time><userid>108107885722943817698<//userid>< review>
While researching new wineries to try on our latest Napa trip I decided to give Cosentino a try.  They're right off of St. Helena highway so depending on the traffic and direction you are travelling it can be a bit of a pain getting in and out of their parking lot.  We tried a few of their reds and the one that I liked and ended up buying is The Poet, a nice little blend of Cab, Merlot, Cab Franc, Malbec, and Petit Verdot.  The tasting room was empty when we arrived which is always nice.  The patio out front also looks like a nice place to relax and hang out.

If you join their wine club you get tastings at quite a few other affiliated wineries one of them being B.R. Cohn.  Luckily I recognized the Cohn label as one of the ones that my printing company does.  I mentioned this to the gentlemen who helped us and he waived our tasting fee as I am "in the industry".  I always forget to mention this.  I really need to remember to bring business cards with me when I go to Napa.

We also sampled their Cigar Zin which I really liked as well.  But they were only selling that one by the case as they are trying to get rid of them in order to change the label.  $99 for 12 bottles of wine is a hell of a deal but my wine fridge is already full and I didn't know what I would do with that much wine.  We left only buying the one bottle of Poet and I had been kicking myself ever since.  I mentioned this to one of my co-workers who is into wine and he recommended putting the case in the crawl space under my house.  So I called Cosentino yesterday and ordered a case of the Cigar Zin!  Can't wait until it arrives.</review>

< Review>
I purchased a NewAir Wine Refrigerator from Amazon.  I received the unit with a broken shelf and the door would not seal properly.  I also received extra parts in the unit and missing other parts needed to reverse the door swing.   I called NewAir and they requested a copy of my receipt and pictures of the damages.

Upon receipt of the pictures, NewAir emailed me that they would send me the replacement parts but would require $16.95 in shipping and handling fees.  I contested this as the unit is brand new and was delivered to me damaged.  I should not be required to pay shipping and handling fees for a new unit which was delivered to me damaged.

Stephan at NewAir informed me that I needed to leave feedback on three websites before he could waive the fee.  He provided three links and this was one of them.

I am giving NewAir two stars as thus far I have received a damaged unit and need to jump through hoops for NewAir to stand behind their product.  I hope I receive my replacement parts without further hurdles.

Respectfully, Jennifer<//Review>

<Review>Excellent Customer Service!  My wife and I purchased a 46 bottle dual zone wine cooler from Amazon.  It arrived in great condition. Although I unwrapped it from the box, I kept it in the bottom tray of the box so it wouldn't scratch our floors when moving it.  The new counter is finally completed and I went to remove the cooler from the bottom box and the bolts meant to secure the compressor fell out. <Resp>None</Resp><Text>I am not sure why I was sent a request to do a survey, but ok.  I ordered a CC100H from the website and I discovered that you could save a few dollars by ordering a "blemished model".  So I ordered a CC-100H from the site and the transaction was smooth, shipping was rather quick.  I do live close to the New Air factory in Cypress, CA so I didn't expect shipping to take long at all.  I got my CC-100H delivered to the house and I didn't get home until late last night.  I opened the box eagerly to see what was inside, and how bad the "blemish" was.

To my surprise the only "blemish" I could find was the front wood of the Cedar drawer has some spots that were in the wood, like sap.  Totally natural imperfections in the wood.  Nothing humanly wrong with the unit.  I was relieved.  Mind you this was like 10 pm, and I quickly got to work cleaning out the interior, placing a box of baking soda in there, got it all set up, turned on the unit, and it ran fine, and I went to bed.

This morning I got up, I smelled the interior of the unit and it smelled like cedar and not plastic, so I decided to grab all of the cedar parts and get them seasoned up and put them in the unit, to season while I was at work today.   Today was also trash day, so I took the box and the Styrofoam and put them in the trash like a good husband would do on trash day.  When I broke the box down I looked at the model number on the box and saw it said "Model CC-100".  I hopped in the car and began my trek to work.  I was thinking about this and I wondered, if New Air sent me the wrong unit.  So I called my wife and asked her to photo that box again, (before the trash guys got to it) and to take a photo of the back of my New air unit that was at the house.  Sure enough...I was sent a CC100 and not the heated version CC-100H as I ordered.

I got to work and I checked my invoice, and sure enough, I ordered the CC-100H Blemished.  So I shot an email off to sales and I told them of the error.  They responded super fast and said I can send it back, but they are all out of the CC100H.  I told them that would not be practical as I have told them the above story, I trashed the packing material and all and the box is now gone.  I asked why in the world would you send me the cc100 if that is not what I ordered?

Here is the response:

Hi Paul,
‚Äã
Thank you for the response, the unit is out of stock I am not sure as to why the wrong unit was sent without confronting you about it first. I am sorry the inconvenience Can you confirm if you will stay with the unit you received?

Thank you,

Stephan
Customer Service Representative

Soooo....I am not sure what I expect them to do...pick it up and bring me out a new one?  No way.  Do I expect they will, send me a replacement for the correct one I bought, and a return label to ship the other one back??  Possibly, but they do not have the unit in stock to do that, and I did buy a Blemished model...so would they need to charge me more for a new "perfect" cc-100H? That wasn't even discussed in the short email, I posted above.  What about discounting me the price I paid since the model is wrong?  Nope, I don't expect that because I already got a great discount.

Am I going to ship it back?  I'm not.  I already cleaned the unit, seasoned it and got it all in the spot where I want it at the house.  The point is, I did not get what I ordered.  My inquiry to the company was responded to quickly, but no creative solution was even offered to make it right.  I guess at this point I would have accepted, "I looked at your order, and you are right, we totally messed that up.  I talked to "so and so" in shipping and told them of this error, and this will not happen again.  So sorry, what can we do to make this right for you?"

In the response above, he came close.  But close does not always make the mark.  Bottom line..I have a nice humidor, it just does not heat....sorry I rambled..but you asked, and I answered.< /Text>< Gmap_id>

<user_id>117585301701937690263< /user_id><Time>1536804471588</Time>< Review>
I purchased a New Air 32 bottle dual zone wine refrigerator (AW-321ED) nearly a year ago. I gradually became frustrated with it, though, because one side was not keeping the temperature. I kept trying to remember to look into the problem, but life got in the way, as it does. The other night I saw the temperature on one side was up to 60 degrees, while the setting was for 49! That spurred me on. So I went right to my computer and found a number and called customer support the next day.
Kenmar, with their customer service, walked me through what to do to troubleshoot the problem. I was pleased to find that it was a damaged cooler kit in the unit and Kenmar told me that they would replace it and it would only cost me $8 shipping. (Way better than shipping the whole unit back to them! Something I'd feared.) Now the plug and "play" replacement part is on its way. I was very pleasantly surprised by the simplicity of the solution and hope that I no longer have trouble with the unit once the new cooling kit gets installed. I suspect that will be the case, since the other side of the unit has been fine. Thanks to Kenmar, I was pretty glad I finally called their support line.< /Review>

<date>1536804471588<//date><rating>4<//rating>< Text>
I purchased a New Air 32 bottle dual zone wine refrigerator (AW-321ED) nearly a year ago. I gradually became frustrated with it, though, because one side was not keeping the temperature. I kept trying to remember to look into the problem, but life got in the way, as it does. The other night I saw the temperature on one side was up to 60 degrees, while the setting was for 49! That spurred me on. So I went right to my computer and found a number and called customer support the next day.
Kenmar, with their customer service, walked me through what to do to troubleshoot the problem. I was pleased to find that it was a damaged cooler kit in the unit and Kenmar told me that they would replace it and it would only cost me $8 shipping. (Way better than shipping the whole unit back to them! Something I'd feared.) Now the plug and "play" replacement part is on its way. I was very pleasantly surprised by the simplicity of the solution and hope that I no longer have trouble with the unit once the new cooling kit gets installed. I suspect that will be the case, since the other side of the unit has been fine. Thanks to Kenmar, I was pretty glad I finally called their support line.< /Text>

< Review>
I recently purchased a AW-281E wine cooler and after 3 months experienced a problem with the unit not reducing temperature. The unit had been running at a constant 54 degrees without issue since purchase. When I called customer service, I was greeted by Genefer who was extremely helpful in helping me resolve my problem. After describing my problem, she was quickly able to diagnose the problem and recommended a new cooling unit. She also indicated that it could be installed quickly and easily with directions that would be emailed out (which I received quickly). Genefer was a pleasure to deal with and provided exemplary customer service. I was relieved when I found out that the parts would be covered free of charge given my recent purchase. The store I purchased the unit at was less than helpful, so this was certainly a relief. I am very happy with my NewAir purchase and commitment to their products and customer service, as well as the wonderful customer service Genefer provided me.< /Review>
